<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d6c3bf22-88d3-4fd1-b15d-7e0bee669780'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer13449416248007129617"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/523268.gif' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>OH MY SWEET GOODNESS. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/481787.gif' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>ALEXANDRA BRACKEN, WHAT HAVE YOU DONE TO ME?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429558ra/860657.gif' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>So let me start off by saying that this novella is 90 pages, including the preview of NEVER FADE. Those 90 pages happen to be the most stressful and emotional 90 pages I have ever read. <br/><br/>The main character in this novella isn't even in THE DARKEST MINDS. Which disappointed me at first, because I was really hoping for a Liam story. But the protagonist is a new character named Gabriel, who wants to become a skip tracer. And after r</span>
  <span id="freeText13449416248007129617" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/523268.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>OH MY SWEET GOODNESS. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/481787.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>ALEXANDRA BRACKEN, WHAT HAVE YOU DONE TO ME?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429558ra/860657.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>So let me start off by saying that this novella is 90 pages, including the preview of NEVER FADE. Those 90 pages happen to be the most stressful and emotional 90 pages I have ever read. <br><br>The main character in this novella isn't even in THE DARKEST MINDS. Which disappointed me at first, because I was really hoping for a Liam story. But the protagonist is a new character named Gabriel, who wants to become a skip tracer. And after reading the first few pages...<br><br>I HATED HIM!<br><br>He is awful. He calls the kids freaks, and has no respect for them, AND I JUST HATED HIM! HE IS SUCH A JERK!<br><br>Then a certain character shows up, and I about cry. <br><br>And the rest of the novella, I was right on the edge of tears the whole time. So many emotions!<br><br>Then the ending came.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/601580.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I cried so hard! In just, like, 70 pages I had gotten so attached to the characters and the story, and the ending made me bawl. <br><br>I thought it couldn't get any worse. So, I read the preview of NEVER FADE, and I felt like this. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429558ra/860658.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't I just can't. <br><br>I NEED NEVER FADE SO BAD!!!<br><br>In short, one of the best and most emotional 90 pages I have ever read. <br><br>Ever. <br><br>Thank you, Miss Bracken, for writing such an amazing novella to tide me over until NEVER FADE comes out. I cannot wait!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2950988158836463791">My heart just broke into a thousand pieces. I can’t believe what just happened. This is one of the best novellas I have ever read. I have no words to describe what I’m feeling. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ I just met Gabe and after those hundred pages, he just DIED. I have no words to describe what I’m feeling. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I just met Gabe and after those hundred pages, he just DIED. WHY!?!?! My heart is broken because he can’t just die like that.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> This book was short but it made me so emotional and right now I’m sobbing, I just can’t believe it. Other than the tragedy that just happened I finally got to met Zu again considering she isn’t in the second book. I missed her a lot. I'm so glad to know she is safe. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Before I read this novella I saw some reviews and they said the ending was sad so the whole time I though Zu was going to die so I was waiting for it but then…but then Gabe’s death just comes out of nowhere and slaps you in the face. Gabe really changed and decided to help Zu and to start to help other kids. His opinion changed about them. He could have helped so many children.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Even though its been like 10 minutes since I finished the novella, I am still heartbroken. This novella was perfect and I was able to really feel something for a character that I only read about for a small period of time.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1690500700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16337746212098968974">I don't think I can possibly write a full review for a novella but I just want to say -- <i>what the heck</i>? That ending crushed my heart and the whole process of seeing inside someone who is not a kid with powers was so engaging. I couldn't put it down once I was given time to read. Seeing Zu as well filled my heart, but damn Gabe turned out to be a great protagonist. If you're reading this series, I would without a doubt recommend this novella!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44487975-dannii-elle?shelf=fantastic-fabrications">fantastic-fabrications</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1745194476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1687994187825691960">This novella follows from the first book in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_' title='The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Minds</a> trilogy. At just under 100 pages I wasn't really expecting a lot, but wow. Bracken really knows how to write a novella!<br/><br/>This is centered around Gabe's perspective, a character not featured in the original series. Gabe represents the average American citizen, attempting to struggle through the economic repression that has ripped through America in the wake of the mutant abilities suddenly conjured in almost all teenage and pre-teen chil</span>
  <span id="freeText1687994187825691960" style="display:none">This novella follows from the first book in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_" title="The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Minds</a> trilogy. At just under 100 pages I wasn't really expecting a lot, but wow. Bracken really knows how to write a novella!<br /><br />This is centered around Gabe's perspective, a character not featured in the original series. Gabe represents the average American citizen, attempting to struggle through the economic repression that has ripped through America in the wake of the mutant abilities suddenly conjured in almost all teenage and pre-teen children. An old knee injury means he cannot join the forces controlling these 'freaks' and there is little place left for him in society: he is a collateral victim in this futuristic community. His subsequent hatred for the 'freaks' that caused his current state is almost palpable. That is, until a small, mute 'yellow' makes his acquaintance...<br /><br />Whilst short, this managed to incorporate a well-rounded story, featuring characters both new and beloved, in a well-formulated world. The action and intrigue was kept at a maximum, and there were so many places where I was reading this with my heart in my mouth. This is a great addition to the series, providing further details to the main plot, as well as maintaining itself as a single spin-off story.</span>

<div id="review_675084519" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/675084519" />
    <a title="Mitch" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8170554-mitch"><img alt="Mitch" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396208595p2/8170554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/675084519?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mitch" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mitch" href="/user/show/8170554-mitch">Mitch</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer675084519" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15178856317706267856">Apparently my problem with <i>The Darkest Minds</i> was just Ruby and Liam, because I really like this short story with Gabe and Zu. As I said (in a review I didn't expect to be as controversial as it's turned out), this is a series that excels at gritty dystopian - or it would be, if it didn't spend so much time making Ruby out to be this weak, self-loathing victim in a black and white adults versus kids world; it was all just a bit too much for me the way the book blatantly tried to play every. singl</span>
  <span id="freeText15178856317706267856" style="display:none">Apparently my problem with <i>The Darkest Minds</i> was just Ruby and Liam, because I really like this short story with Gabe and Zu. As I said (in a review I didn't expect to be as controversial as it's turned out), this is a series that excels at gritty dystopian - or it would be, if it didn't spend so much time making Ruby out to be this weak, self-loathing victim in a black and white adults versus kids world; it was all just a bit too much for me the way the book blatantly tried to play every. single. emotion. card. ever. (Nor did the meandering plot help.) Anyway though, <i>In Time</i> is different; it's a great companion that adds exactly the perspective I thought was missing from the first book - that of the reluctant bounty hunter who's supposed to be on the trail of these kids (Gabe). Sure, his reasons are a bit trite (the economy tanked; he's in it for the money) and I probably liked his character for mostly the wrong reasons (think of kids like dogs! you're just returning them to the pound!) but you know the whole thing is, in a way, absurd, and I really like his side of things (even if that kind of absurdity and dark humor may not have been intentional) as opposed to Ruby's whole 'woe is me!' thing she's got going (yeah, I know it's a natural reaction to being locked up the way she was, but I just thought the book for fiction was trying too hard in that regard). Plus, this story addresses a whole bunch of flaws from the original setup (not perfectly, but still) - how the color coding came to be, what's going on with the parents on the outside, etc., Zu's pretty great as usual, and heck, even the ending, while in the same style as <i>The Darkest Minds</i>, worked for me because I actually liked these characters (let's just say no good deed goes unpunished). All in all, pretty good for an original short story and I'm definitely glad this isn't another weak rehash as many tie in novellas have been recently. Still have zero interest in Ruby and Liam (sorry), but this was great.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15178856317706267856" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1209665624" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1209665624" />
    <a title="Dana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7632558-dana"><img alt="Dana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522963716p2/7632558.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1209665624?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dana" href="/user/show/7632558-dana">Dana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=buy">buy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=up-all-night">up-all-night</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=childrens">childrens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=young-adult-paranormal">young-adult-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7632558-dana?shelf=short-story">short-story</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1209665624" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer623785685802936029"><br/>Wow...that's how you write a novella! I really appreciated that this was a true sequel and not a random prequel. I love back story as much as the next person, but sometimes you just want story 1.5 to actually be story 1.5, so thank you for that Ms. Bracken. <br/><br/>I was riveted while reading this and yet, to be honest I despised Gabe. I can't remember the last time I cursed a character so much. <b>But</b> the writing was so good and the story was so interesting that even with my hatred for the main character,</span>
  <span id="freeText623785685802936029" style="display:none"><br />Wow...that's how you write a novella! I really appreciated that this was a true sequel and not a random prequel. I love back story as much as the next person, but sometimes you just want story 1.5 to actually be story 1.5, so thank you for that Ms. Bracken. <br /><br />I was riveted while reading this and yet, to be honest I despised Gabe. I can't remember the last time I cursed a character so much. <b>But</b> the writing was so good and the story was so interesting that even with my hatred for the main character, I still loved this addition to the Darkest Minds collection. <br /><br /><b>Buy, Borrow or Bin Verdict:</b> For $0.79 I would say this story is definitely worth a <b>Buy</b>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="623785685802936029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=dark-atmosphere">dark-atmosphere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=huge-character-development">huge-character-development</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=good-vs-bad">good-vs-bad</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692335065" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7510974014248102365">This little tidbit depicts the world Bracken previously introduced us to perfectly. Focused on a new character, Gabe -- a collateral victim of the scary universe the author has created -- is trying to take the reins to his crumbling world and join the skip tracers. But for his big debut, he needs to turn a "freak kid" in. And that somehow proves a thousand times easier and harder (trust me, I do make sense) than he initially thought. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>“But I’m telling you now, you ever find someone who likes t</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText7510974014248102365" style="display:none">This little tidbit depicts the world Bracken previously introduced us to perfectly. Focused on a new character, Gabe -- a collateral victim of the scary universe the author has created -- is trying to take the reins to his crumbling world and join the skip tracers. But for his big debut, he needs to turn a "freak kid" in. And that somehow proves a thousand times easier and harder (trust me, I do make sense) than he initially thought. <br><br><i>
  <b>“But I’m telling you now, you ever find someone who likes the job, you better goddamn run the other way because you’re looking at the real monster. You’re looking right at him.”</b>
</i><br><br>Gabe is half an egocentric douchebag, half a broken boy who lost his way. Fortunately, his character development is oh-so-wonderful and the guy grew on me. But this transformation happens gradually thanks to one of the cutest characters ever, who I already loved from the first installment -- happy would be an understatement to describe my feelings when I finally got what's happening. <br><br>Ending on a high note that triggered my sobbing and instant desire to start <i>Never Fade</i>, this novella is a great tease of things to come. I really hope its plotline will be developed further in the sequel, because you cannot leave me hanging like that.<br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-i5qzlNcx_dI/VSLFF5Uo7nI/AAAAAAAAOxo/G5VcCQVyktM/s1600/7144475.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428342170ra/14408436.gif" height="160" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Also, there was a scene that got the sudden "omg" reaction from me -- it didn't have a key role in the story, but it unraveled another piece of TDM's puzzle, which I always crave for. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HPE7DsFs0_4/VSLFEnkqyMI/AAAAAAAAOxg/I-n6ELb2W8o/s1600/tumblr_mxz6kf7m6m1qft49to1_500.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428342170ra/14408437.gif" height="143" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This being said, I honestly don't know if <i>In Time</i> is mandatory in order to get the gist of following events, but I enjoyed it tremendously so I don't see any point in not reading it. Plus, you get some more time with that awesome character I've mentioned and that's enough of a reason for you to read this novella. <br><br><b>ENJOY! &lt;3</b></span>

<div id="review_1732611291" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1732611291" />
    <a title="Marnie  (Enchanted Bibliophile)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6108495-marnie-enchanted-bibliophile"><img alt="Marnie  (Enchanted Bibliophile)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450344827p2/6108495.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1732611291?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marnie  (Enchanted Bibliophile)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marnie  (Enchanted Bibliophile)" href="/user/show/6108495-marnie-enchanted-bibliophile">Marnie  (Enchanted Bibliophile)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6108495-marnie-enchanted-bibliophile?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6108495-marnie-enchanted-bibliophile?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6108495-marnie-enchanted-bibliophile?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1732611291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1421366900536194435">In January I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_' title='The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Minds</a> and immediately ordered the rest of the books. I fell in love with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2973783.Alexandra_Bracken' title='Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alexandra Bracken</a>'s writing style and with this dystopian world she created, but as things go I didn't get around to reading the rest of the series up until now.<br/><br/>I'm glad I saw that there's a connector story between <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_' title='The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Darkest Minds</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150830.Never_Fade__The_Darkest_Minds___2_' title='Never Fade (The Darkest Minds, #2) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>Never Fade</a>, because this novella was just what I needed to get back into this world and the characters that inhabit it.<br/><br/>So now I'm ready for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150830.Never_Fade__The_Darkest_Minds___2_' title='Never Fade (The Darkest Minds, #2) by Alexandra Bracken' rel='nofollow noopener'>Never Fade</a>. Hopefull</span>
  <span id="freeText1421366900536194435" style="display:none">In January I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_" title="The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Minds</a> and immediately ordered the rest of the books. I fell in love with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2973783.Alexandra_Bracken" title="Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">Alexandra Bracken</a>'s writing style and with this dystopian world she created, but as things go I didn't get around to reading the rest of the series up until now.<br /><br />I'm glad I saw that there's a connector story between <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10576365.The_Darkest_Minds__The_Darkest_Minds___1_" title="The Darkest Minds (The Darkest Minds, #1) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">The Darkest Minds</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150830.Never_Fade__The_Darkest_Minds___2_" title="Never Fade (The Darkest Minds, #2) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">Never Fade</a>, because this novella was just what I needed to get back into this world and the characters that inhabit it.<br /><br />So now I'm ready for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150830.Never_Fade__The_Darkest_Minds___2_" title="Never Fade (The Darkest Minds, #2) by Alexandra Bracken" rel="nofollow noopener">Never Fade</a>. Hopefully I can get started with it today still.</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=evul-people-are-evul">evul-people-are-evul</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer682200183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer659642861203472741"><b>2.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br/><br/><i>In Time</i> was much better than I thought it'd be, though that's not saying much since I find most novellas rubbish. <br/>This was more enjoyable than <i>The Darkest Mind</i>, mainly because the POV character wasn't quite as insufferable as Ruby or whatever her name was. Although, I would have preferred to read the POV of an existing character (like Zu or Liam) instead of some random guy. <br/>I didn't really like Gabe (the MC) at first, he was kind of awful. But by the end, I did grow to like h</span>
  <span id="freeText659642861203472741" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br /><br /><i>In Time</i> was much better than I thought it'd be, though that's not saying much since I find most novellas rubbish. <br />This was more enjoyable than <i>The Darkest Mind</i>, mainly because the POV character wasn't quite as insufferable as Ruby or whatever her name was. Although, I would have preferred to read the POV of an existing character (like Zu or Liam) instead of some random guy. <br />I didn't really like Gabe (the MC) at first, he was kind of awful. But by the end, I did grow to like him — he had quite a bit of character growth considering how short a read it was. It was sad how insecure, desperate and alone Gabe was - I actually understood why he was initially willing to capture and imprison a psi kid. He had no friends, no money and no hope, and he was left behind by everyone… So yea, his attitude made sense. Even though Gabe did improve as a character, he was still rather boring. I guess he did make a nice change from the usual arrogant male POV though.<br />I enjoyed Zu's character, she was one of the very few I could stand in <i>The Darkest Minds.</i> Her interactions with Gabe were actually quite sweet. Also, I loved her reaction to watching <i>Wizard of Oz.</i><br />The ending was quite sad with Gabe dying after he finally found something worth doing. I'm hoping that he ends up surviving, so he can help Zu and co avoid capture.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="659642861203472741" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_737684688" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/737684688" />
    <a title="Julie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16529168-julie"><img alt="Julie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485395880p2/16529168.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737684688?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie" href="/user/show/16529168-julie">Julie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16529168-julie?shelf=books-i-own-ebook">books-i-own-ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16529168-julie?shelf=need-to-buy-print">need-to-buy-print</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16529168-julie?shelf=2013-dystopian-bc">2013-dystopian-bc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737684688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9937652103819893721"><b>
  <i>“Sometimes the darkness lives inside you, and sometimes it wins.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>This e-novella follows up from Bracken's previous novel The Darkest Minds, and just like that book, this short story practically tore me up on the inside. <br/><br/>It focuses on a young man named Gabe who, due to the economic crisis that followed the discovery of children with unnatural abilities is struggling. His only option to try and make something of his life is to become a skip tracer, a hunter of children who managed to escape th</span>
  <span id="freeText9937652103819893721" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“Sometimes the darkness lives inside you, and sometimes it wins.”</i>
</b><br /><br />This e-novella follows up from Bracken's previous novel The Darkest Minds, and just like that book, this short story practically tore me up on the inside. <br /><br />It focuses on a young man named Gabe who, due to the economic crisis that followed the discovery of children with unnatural abilities is struggling. His only option to try and make something of his life is to become a skip tracer, a hunter of children who managed to escape the system in place to 'protect' them. However, his first catch, a little girl named Suzume who doesn't talk will make his job difficult, and lead him to realise that the government's involvement is not all as it seems. <br /><br />Zu was one of my favourite character's in The Darkest Minds so you can imagine my joy when I figured out that she was in this novella. The relationship Bracken manages to build between the two main character's is heart-wrenching and the dangers they both face together, provide a riveting journey of self-preservation and growth that will keep you coming back for more. This just increased my anticipation for Never Fade and love Bracken even more. <br /><br />I would recommend this to all fans of dystopia, YA and those who love a fast-paced plot with wonderfully fleshed out characters. I applaud Bracken's ability to evoke so much emotion from me in less than 150 pages and I would just like to reiterate just how much I enjoyed this book. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9937652103819893721" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_672819966" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/672819966" />
    <a title="Jenny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7004681-jenny"><img alt="Jenny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376679883p2/7004681.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/672819966?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny" href="/user/show/7004681-jenny">Jenny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer672819966" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7666233539705084103">If you've read the Darkest Minds - GO READ THIS! I usually don't have very high expectations when it comes to "half-books" because they normally just give you more insight on a story you already know, but this... oh man...! The story is a bit slow in the beginning, it follows a guy named Gabe who wants to get out of town and decides to become a skip tracer in order to earn money. <br/>Although I found the Darkest Mind rather predictable, everything in this novella was just really unexpected. This mad</span>
  <span id="freeText7666233539705084103" style="display:none">If you've read the Darkest Minds - GO READ THIS! I usually don't have very high expectations when it comes to "half-books" because they normally just give you more insight on a story you already know, but this... oh man...! The story is a bit slow in the beginning, it follows a guy named Gabe who wants to get out of town and decides to become a skip tracer in order to earn money. <br />Although I found the Darkest Mind rather predictable, everything in this novella was just really unexpected. This made me really excited again to read Never Fade!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7666233539705084103" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/994316450?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rache" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rache" href="/user/show/4985646-rache">Rache</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4985646-rache?shelf=cried-properly">cried-properly</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4985646-rache?shelf=female-power">female-power</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4985646-rache?shelf=damn-you-cliffhanger">damn-you-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4985646-rache?shelf=novellas-short-stories">novellas-short-stories</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer994316450" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5576178173915753591">More of a <b>★ 3.75 ★</b><br/><br/>I have to admit I was a little disappointed by finding out this didn't have something to do with the main characters. That's why I didn't got much into the story as I wanted to. <br/>But I still kept reading because <b>Alexandra Bracken.</b> Besides, it was interesting to read from a totally different POV. Gabe's thoughts were entertaining and I ended up liking him.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I guess I just assumed the only financial gain was in turning kids in, not, you know, returning them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>That got me</span>
  <span id="freeText5576178173915753591" style="display:none">More of a <b>★ 3.75 ★</b><br><br>I have to admit I was a little disappointed by finding out this didn't have something to do with the main characters. That's why I didn't got much into the story as I wanted to. <br>But I still kept reading because <b>Alexandra Bracken.</b> Besides, it was interesting to read from a totally different POV. Gabe's thoughts were entertaining and I ended up liking him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I guess I just assumed the only financial gain was in turning kids in, not, you know, returning them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>That got me thinking <i>"What if there were good skip tracers? That instead of making a kid's life miserable, helped them get back to where they would like to?"</i> I never thought about that, and it's completely helpful. People like Gabe are an example.<br><br>Back to the story, coincidentally, the little kid Gabe's going to use to become a skip tracer turns out to be <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Zu<br><br>I WAS SO HAPPY BECAUSE I MISSED HER A LOT AND I NEEDED SOME OF HER CUTENESS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419134313i/12998947.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I did got a little confused because I read <i>Never Fade</i> before this, so at first, I don't know why, I thought these events were happening before the first book. But then remembered she got away with some friends at the end of the first book. And you know what else I remembered? <b>Liam's note</b><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>“With it in hand, Liam knelt down in front of Zu and tore off half the sheet of paper Kylie had given him. I wished I could have seen what he had written there, but it wasn't for my eyes. When he was finished, he folded the paper over several times and pressed it into her palm”</i></b> <i><br>-The Darkest Minds</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Since that happened, I thought the note Zu had was the one Liam gave her. And then one lady who helps kids starts saying she has two sons and keeps stating that. <i>Suspicious</i><br><br>AND THEN<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“We love you. If you need help, look for my parents—they're using the names Della and Jim Goodkind—and tell them I sent you”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <u>THE NOTE.</u><br><br><b>Time I figured out I just met my mother-in-law.</b><br><br>Moving on; what is it with Alexandra and endings? Seriously. Those are always the best, <s>which leave you crying like a baby whale.</s><br>There’s no book of hers I haven’t cried reading. Good job, <i>I guess?</i><br><br>The only reason I'm not giving this a five star is because it was hard for me to start. That's it. Oh, and the ending; right. <i>Why would you?</i><br>I TRUSTED YOU, BRACKEN. <b>I TRUSTED YOU.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385345804ra/7130180.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[So many questions unanswered. First, this is one I forgot to ask in the first book; I didn't get that part... Is there another Ruby Daly? I mean, does Ruby have a sister?!<br>Second, DOES ZU HAVE A TWIN OR WHAT? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Qs3ao3rwUWeHDfty2QByigqUftAw7adG2D0EdGJ3fFOoMC6CGa1hghPKUi4+ql5QrSOXam/xqqmEOYWmTM0EfA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mscTLAi+xaRrxRbOCDIpFNhxL7ocSfY+4PQPu/E/sZpwOucNa+P1Qf8Cv5LvmAXOf8bGAENV+9G88I5p34XJtQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
